## Diagram 2

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Test as test_remove_duplicate_milestones
    participant Fixture as sample_update_events
    participant Mapping as PackageContainerSearchPostgresqlMappingBase
    
    Test->>Fixture: Get sample events
    Fixture-->>Test: Return 5 events (with 1 duplicate)
    Test->>Mapping: Create instance(version="test", is_async_export=False)
    Test->>Mapping: remove_duplicate_milestones(sample_update_events)
    Mapping->>Mapping: Process event list
    Mapping->>Mapping: Remove duplicate milestone events
    Mapping-->>Test: Return 4 unique events
    Test->>Test: Assert isinstance(result, list)
    Test->>Test: Assert len(result) == 4
```
